### **1. Analysis Breakdown: The Signature of Precision**

Our statistical models have identified highly unusual patterns of play within this game, indicative of external assistance.

*   **Near-Perfect Engine Correlation (Temperature MLE: 0.035):** This player's move choices exhibit an astonishingly low softmax temperature, practically zero. This metric quantifies how closely a player's moves align with the engine's top choices. A value of 0.035 suggests an almost perfect, machine-like correlation, where the player consistently selected the engine's absolute best move with virtually no deviation.
*   **Unnaturally Precise Play (Lambda MLE: 63.74):** The exponential rate parameter for winrate loss is exceptionally high, far exceeding the threshold for human play. This indicates an almost negligible loss in winrate per move, a level of precision typically only achievable by a powerful Gomoku engine.
*   **Overwhelming Statistical Evidence (Log Likelihood Ratio: 15.59):** The Log Likelihood Ratio strongly favors the cheater model over the human model by a factor of over 15. This metric provides compelling statistical evidence that the observed play patterns are significantly more likely to originate from a cheating agent than a human player.
*   **Consistent Optimal Decision-Making (Near-Optimal Pct: 69.6% & Mean Delta: 1.51%):** Nearly 70% of this player's moves resulted in a winrate loss of less than 2%, with an average winrate loss of just 1.51% per move. Furthermore, the "good player" component of their move distribution (em_lambda_good: 9997.98) shows an almost infinite lambda, signifying near-perfect play for a significant portion of the game.

### **2. Context & History: A Consistent Pattern**

*   **Immediate Engine-Like Play (CUSUM Triggered: Yes, Change Point: 1):** A significant shift in play strength was detected, indicating a change in the player's performance. Crucially, this shift occurred at **move 1**, meaning the player exhibited engine-like precision and consistency from the very opening of the game, rather than toggling a bot mid-match.
*   **Historical Precedent (Profile History: SUSPICIOUS, Z-Score/T-Stat: 8.31, Historical Lambda: 29.09):** The player's historical profile already flags them as "SUSPICIOUS" with a significantly high Z-Score/T-Stat and a high historical Lambda, reinforcing the pattern of unusually strong and precise play across multiple games.

### **3. Final Verdict**

**Classification: Suspicious (LRT-flagged)**
This player is statistically flagged as suspicious due to overwhelming evidence of engine-like precision, near-perfect move correlation, and consistent optimal play from the very start of the game.

### **4. Referee's Advice**

While the Bayesian posterior probability of cheating (`p_cheat`) is 28.3%, the sheer weight and consistency of the other advanced metrics present a far more compelling case. The extremely low `temperature_mle` (0.035), the exceptionally high `lambda_mle` (63.74), and the `log_lr` (15.59) which strongly favors the cheater model, are all critical indicators that override a potentially conservative `p_cheat` value in this specific instance.
